 ) Before the six-day army recruitment rally in Mhow, Madhya Pradesh, starting April 25, the army has given special instructions to the candidates regarding the scale of tattoo (tattooing)
 iske mutabik agar kisi ummidavaar ke baaju ke nichle hisse ke alaava sharir ke duusare ang par tatu paaya jaataa he to use raily ke liye ayogy mana jaayegaa
 Colonel GS Daveta, director of Mhow's Army Recruiting Office, told reporters here today, "as per the instructions of the Army Headquarters, we will disqualify a candidate who has a lower arm (the middle part of the wrist and elbow) for the recruitment rally
 Have a name, symbol or religious symbol tattooed on the other part
 ’ He told, 'if a candidate has tattooed on the lower side of his arm, he will be considered eligible to participate in the army recruitment rally
 ’ daveta ne vistrut byora diye bagaiyr bataaya, ‘sena bhartee raily main shaamil hone vaale kuch ummidavaar aids ke marij paye gayi, jinhone apane sharir main tatu kara rakhe the
 In view of this, a scale has been set in relation to tattoos for recruitment rally
 ’ tippaniyan Daveta said, 'it has been seen that many people are tattooed by piercing a single needle, especially in rural areas
 isse aids jaisi ghaatak beemaari failane kaa khatra rahata he
 Secondly, tattoo makers in these areas are neither trained, nor are their tools safe
 ’ daveta ne bataaya ki yahaan se kareeb 25 kilometre dur mau main agle maheene hone vaale bhartee raily pashchimi madhyapradesh ke indore or ujjain sambhaagon ke yuvaaon ke liye yojit kii ja rahi he

 unhone bataaya, ‘agar kisi ummidavaar ne apane baaju ke nichle hisse bhar main tatu karaayaa he to use sena bhartee raily main bhaag lene ke yogya mana jaayegaa

" ise dekhte hue bhartee raily ke liye tatu ke sambandh main paimaana tay kiya gaya he
 Comments daveta ne kaha, ‘aisa dekha gaya he ki khaskar gramin kshetron main ek hi sui chubhokar kai logon ko tatu kiya jaataa he
 This puts the risk of spreading a deadly disease like AIDS
 duusare, in kshetron main tatu banane vaale log na to prashikshit hote hai, na hi unke aujaar surakshit hote hai

 ) Ichawar assembly seat of Madhya Pradesh falls in Sehore district
 ichhaavar rajdhani bhopal se 57 kimi kii duuri par sthit he
 It is the seatbjp's stronghold, though it lost in the 2013 election
 ichhaavar ke bare main ek or baat khaas he
 It is said that the Chief Minister who visits Ichhawar has to lose his chair
 or itihaas bhi kuch aisa hi bataata he
 You can guess from this that Shivraj Singh himself, as CM, has not come to its area
 bataa den ichhaavar ke myth ko todane kaa prayaas kai mukhyamantri kar chuke hai, lekin jitne bhi mukhyamantriyon ne yahaan kadam rakhaa un sabhi ko apni kursi ganvaani padi
 In 2003, the then Chief Minister Digvijay Singh also reached Ichawar to break this myth to attend a cooperative conference held on 15 November 2003
 iske baad madhya pradesh main hue chunaavon mencongressko karaari haar kaa saamana karnaa padaa tha
 Trying to break the myth of Ichawar, Chief Minister Dr
 kailash nath katju ne bhi kii thi
 Katju came to Ichawar to participate in a program of assembly elections on 12 January 1962 and after this the Congress lost in the assembly elections held on 11 March 1962 and Dr
 kailash nath katju ko apni satta se hanth dhonaa padaa
 On 1 March 1967, Dwarka Prasad Mishra also came to Ichawar and due to dissatisfaction with the formation of new cabinet on 7 March 1967, Mishra had to resign as Chief Minister
 2013 or 2008 ke chunavi nattejey2013 ke chunaav main congress ke shailandra ramesh chandra patel ne bijepi ke karan singh kanhaiyalaal ko sirf 744 voton se haraaya tha
 In the 2008 election, Karan Singh Verma of BJP, Dr
 of Congress
 balvir tomars ko 18 hajaar se zyada voton se haraaya tha
 Karan Singh Tomar received 50129 votes in this election, while Dr
 balvir tomars 31977 vot mili the
 What were the results of the state in 2013 Madhya Pradesh has a total of 231 assembly seats
 230 siton par chunaav hote hai jabaki ek sadsy ko manonith kiya jaataa he
 In the 2013 elections, BJP got 165 seats, Congress 58, BSP 4 and others three seats

 karnataka main bhartiya janata party (bhaajapa) ko fori raahat to jarur mil gai he lekin uskaa sankat abhi tala nahin he
 Former Chief Minister BS Yeddyurappa, who was adamant on his removal from the post of Chief Minister Sadanand Gowda, announced on Monday that he and his supporters would neither resign from the Assembly nor quit the BJP for the time being
 yediurppa ne jahaan maujuuda sankat ke liye mukhyamantri sadanand gauda or party mahasachiv annat kumaar ko jimmedaar tehraaya vahiin duusari ore kendriya netritv ko apni takat kaa ehsaas karaate hue kaha ki party ke 71 vidhayakon kaa samarthan unhen hasil he or 40 ke istife to unke paas pade hue hai
 Yeddyurappa told reporters here on Monday, "I had decided to leave the party
 yah faisla dopaher 12 baje kaa tha lekin philhal ise main kuch dinon ke liye sthagit kar rahaa hum
 After the appeals of party president Nitin Gadkari, senior leader Arun Jaitley and many religious gurus, we have now deferred the decision to resign and leave the party
 main pradesh bhar main ghumoonga or janata kii raay luungaa
 " yediurppa ne maujuuda sankat ke liye anant kumaar or sadanand gauda ko jimmedaar tehraaya or kaha ki vah iske liye katai jimmedaar nahin hai
 He alleged that the Chief Minister and the state president are constantly insulting him and his supporters, and increasing the drinking with the Janata Dal (secular)
 unhone kaha ki anant kumaar mukhyamantri banane ko betaab hai or gauda sarkaar nahin chalaa sakate
 Yeddyurappa said, "it was because of Ananth Kumar and the gang that he had to step down as Chief Minister
 vah dilli main laalkrishna adwani ko mere khilaaf bargalane kaa kaam karte hai
 "he said that he had received a call from Jaitley and asked him not to take any major decision
 party netaaon ne kaha ki yadi vah istipha de dete hai to party anaath ho jaaegi
 Yeddyurappa said, "I leave it to the central leaders whether they need Yeddyurappa or not
 maine 40 saal party kii seva kii or jab main mukhyamantri bana to bhagyalakshmi or chaatro ko cycle dene kii yojana ko aaj bhi log yaad karte hai
 " yediurppa ne isse pehle daawa kiya ki unhen 71 vidhayakon kaa samarthan hasil he or 40 to abhi istipha dene ko taiyaar he
 Yeddyurappa had said in a press conference in the morning that he would disclose his forward strategy at a press conference at 4 pm
 uske baad aise kayaas lagaae ja rahe the ki yediurppa apane samarthakon ke saath party chhodane kii ghoshnaa kar sakate hai
 Here, in New Delhi, the Congress ignored the praise of Yeddyurappa's party president Sonia Gandhi, saying she did not need a certificate from anyone
 congress pravaktaa manish tiwari ne kaha, "na to congress party or na hi isaki adhyaksh ko kisi se pramaan-patr lene kii jarurat he
 "he said that BJP came to power in the year 2008 and has been struggling with internal differences since then
 unhone kaha, "mujhe ummid he ki agle aath maheenon main jab rajya main vidhansabha chunaav hone vaale he, janata iskaa dhyaan rakhegi
 "comments yediurppa or bhaajapa netritv ke bich jhagade ko unhone party kaa aantarik maamla bataaya
